## Domain Knowledge (LLM-generated)
**Domain**: chemical reaction kinetics
**Analysis**: This task involves determining the rate law for a chemical reaction where dA_dt is the rate of change of concentration A. In chemical kinetics, the rate typically depends on concentration through power-law or more complex functional forms, and may depend explicitly on time for non-autonomous systems (e.g., photochemical reactions, varying temperature).

**Common formula structures in this domain**:
- Zero-order kinetics: dA_dt = c0 (constant rate, independent of concentration)
- First-order kinetics: dA_dt = c0 * A (rate proportional to concentration)
- Second-order kinetics: dA_dt = c0 * A**2 (rate proportional to concentration squared)
- nth-order kinetics: dA_dt = c0 * A**c1 (general power-law rate dependence)
- Mixed order with offset: dA_dt = c0 * A**c1 + c2 (power-law with constant source/sink)
- Reversible first-order: dA_dt = c0 * A + c1 (forward and reverse first-order reactions)
- Michaelis-Menten type: dA_dt = c0 * A / (c1 + A) (enzyme kinetics / saturation kinetics)
- Substrate inhibition: dA_dt = c0 * A / (c1 + A + c2 * A**2) (enzyme kinetics with inhibition)
- Autocatalytic: dA_dt = c0 * A * (c1 + c2 * A) (autocatalytic reaction mechanism)
- Logistic-type rate: dA_dt = c0 * A * (1 + c1 * A) (second-order with linear term)
- Time-dependent first-order: dA_dt = c0 * A * exp(c1 * t) (time-varying rate constant, e.g., temperature ramp)
- Parallel reactions: dA_dt = c0 * A + c1 * A**2 (competing first and second order pathways)
- Fractional order with time: dA_dt = c0 * A**c1 * t**c2 (anomalous kinetics in heterogeneous media)
- Cooperative kinetics: dA_dt = c0 * A**c1 / (c2 + A**c1) (Hill-type cooperative binding/reaction)

**Formula structure heuristic features**:
- Oscillation damping envelope → Exponential decay envelope f(x)*exp(-c*Abs(x)) for symmetric damped oscillation, Gaussian envelope f(x)*exp(-c*x**2) for localized wave packets
- Saturation/clipping effects → Rational fraction x/(1+x), tanh; for variables with alternating positive/negative in oscillatory systems, selectively apply Abs
- Growth/decay → Exponential growth exp(c*t), Logistic 1/(1+exp(-c*x)), power law x**c
- Threshold/activation behavior → Max(x-c, 0), piecewise functions
- Coupling/cross effects → Product terms between variables x*y, power-law coupling x**c1 * y**c2
- Pure concentration dependence without time → classical autonomous rate law (zero, first, second, nth order)
- Rate depends on both A and t explicitly → non-autonomous system suggesting external forcing (temperature change, photochemistry, or diffusion-limited kinetics)
- Rational function of A (numerator/denominator polynomials) → enzyme kinetics or surface catalysis (Langmuir-Hinshelwood mechanism)
- Negative dA_dt values throughout → net consumption/decay of species A
- Sign change of dA_dt as A varies → reversible reaction approaching equilibrium, look for linear terms (c0*A + c1)
- Rate proportional to A*(c0 - A) → autocatalytic or logistic kinetics with a carrying capacity
- Polynomial in A with multiple terms → parallel competing reaction pathways of different orders
- Fractional power of A (A**0.5, A**1.5) → complex reaction mechanisms involving radical intermediates or surface reactions
- Exponential dependence on t → Arrhenius-type temperature programming or photodegradation with varying light intensity
